%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%%\tagged{Cat@One, Cat@Two, Cat@Three, Cat@Four, Cat@Five, Ans@MultiAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Arctrig, Sub@Theorems_MVT}{

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Does the function ${-6 \, \arctan\left(2 \, x\right)}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{5}]$?

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{5})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{2} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(10\right) - 5}{\arctan\left(10\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%




\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Does the function ${-\arctan\left(-10 \, x\right)}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{5}]$?

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{5})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{10} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(50\right) + 5}{\arctan\left(50\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{3}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{3})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{3}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{5} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(15\right) - 3}{\arctan\left(15\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%




%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\begin{problem}

Does the function ${-4 \, \arctan\left(7 \, x\right)}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{4}]$?

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{4}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{4})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{4}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(28\right) - 4}{\arctan\left(28\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Does the function ${4 \, \arctan\left(8 \, x\right)}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{2}]$?

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{2})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{8} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(16\right) - 2}{\arctan\left(16\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0054.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{2})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{4} \, \sqrt{-\frac{\arctan\left(8\right) - 2}{\arctan\left(8\right)}}}\]
\end{problem}}%}
